# History of Present Illness
Helene
 is a 81 year-old non-hispanic black female. Patient has a history of part-time employment (finding), limited social contact (finding), not in labor force (finding), unhealthy alcohol drinking behavior (finding), reports of violence in the environment (finding), full-time employment (finding), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), viral sinusitis (disorder), stress (finding), social isolation (finding).

# Social History
Patient is married. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has NO INSURANCE.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

Patient is married. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet; 24 hr metformin hydrochloride 500 mg extended release oral tablet; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

# Assessment and Plan
Patient is presenting with full-time employment (finding). 

## Plan

The following procedures were conducted:
- assessment of health and social care needs (procedure)
- assessment using morse fall scale (procedure)
- screening for domestic abuse (procedure)
- depression screening (procedure)
- depression screening using patient health questionnaire two-item score (procedure)
- assessment of substance use (procedure)
- assessment using alcohol use disorders identification test - consumption (procedure)
The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]
- hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet
- 24 hr metformin hydrochloride 500 mg extended release oral tablet
- lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet

 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
